\DoxyCodeLine{00350\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00351\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ This\ part\ deals\ with\ the\ special\ case\ where\ a\ unit\ wants\ to\ inline\ xxHash,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00352\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ but\ "{}xxhash.h"{}\ has\ previously\ been\ included\ without\ XXH\_INLINE\_ALL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00353\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ such\ as\ part\ of\ some\ previously\ included\ *.h\ header\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00354\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ Without\ further\ action,\ the\ new\ include\ would\ just\ be\ ignored,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00355\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ and\ functions\ would\ effectively\ \_not\_\ be\ inlined\ (silent\ failure).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00356\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ The\ following\ macros\ solve\ this\ situation\ by\ prefixing\ all\ inlined\ names,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00357\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ avoiding\ naming\ collision\ with\ previous\ inclusions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00358\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00359\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Before\ that,\ we\ unconditionally\ \#undef\ all\ symbols,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00360\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ in\ case\ they\ were\ already\ defined\ with\ XXH\_NAMESPACE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00361\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ They\ will\ then\ be\ redefined\ for\ XXH\_INLINE\_ALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00362\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02060\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02061\ \textcolor{comment}{/*-\/**********************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxHash\ implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *-\/**********************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxHash's\ implementation\ used\ to\ be\ hosted\ inside\ xxhash.c.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02066\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ inlining\ requires\ implementation\ to\ be\ visible\ to\ the\ compiler,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ hence\ be\ included\ alongside\ the\ header.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Previously,\ implementation\ was\ hosted\ inside\ xxhash.c,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ which\ was\ then\ \#included\ when\ inlining\ was\ activated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ construction\ created\ issues\ with\ a\ few\ build\ and\ install\ systems,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ as\ it\ required\ xxhash.c\ to\ be\ stored\ in\ /include\ directory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxHash\ implementation\ is\ now\ directly\ integrated\ within\ xxhash.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ As\ a\ consequence,\ xxhash.c\ is\ no\ longer\ needed\ in\ /include.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02076\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxhash.c\ is\ still\ available\ and\ is\ still\ useful.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ In\ a\ "{}normal"{}\ setup,\ when\ xxhash\ is\ not\ inlined,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02078\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxhash.h\ only\ exposes\ the\ prototypes\ and\ public\ symbols,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ while\ xxhash.c\ can\ be\ built\ into\ an\ object\ file\ xxhash.o}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ which\ can\ then\ be\ linked\ into\ the\ final\ binary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02081\ \textcolor{comment}{\ ************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02082\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02083\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ (\ defined(XXH\_INLINE\_ALL)\ ||\ defined(XXH\_PRIVATE\_API)\ \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02084\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ ||\ defined(XXH\_IMPLEMENTATION)\ )\ \&\&\ !defined(XXH\_IMPLEM\_13a8737387)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02085\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ define\ XXH\_IMPLEM\_13a8737387}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02943\ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ xxh\_u32\ XXH32\_round(xxh\_u32\ acc,\ xxh\_u32\ input)}
\DoxyCodeLine{02944\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02945\ \ \ \ \ acc\ +=\ input\ *\ XXH\_PRIME32\_2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02946\ \ \ \ \ acc\ \ =\ XXH\_rotl32(acc,\ 13);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02947\ \ \ \ \ acc\ *=\ XXH\_PRIME32\_1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02948\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ (defined(\_\_SSE4\_1\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_aarch64\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_wasm\_simd128\_\_))\ \&\&\ !defined(XXH\_ENABLE\_AUTOVECTORIZE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02949\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02950\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ UGLY\ HACK:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02951\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ A\ compiler\ fence\ is\ used\ to\ prevent\ GCC\ and\ Clang\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02952\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ autovectorizing\ the\ XXH32\ loop\ (pragmas\ and\ attributes\ don't\ work\ for\ some}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02953\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ reason)\ without\ globally\ disabling\ SSE4.1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02954\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02955\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ The\ reason\ we\ want\ to\ avoid\ vectorization\ is\ because\ despite\ working\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02956\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ 4\ integers\ at\ a\ time,\ there\ are\ multiple\ factors\ slowing\ XXH32\ down\ on}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03886\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{03887\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03888\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ One\ goal\ of\ XXH3\ is\ to\ make\ it\ fast\ on\ both\ 32-\/bit\ and\ 64-\/bit,\ while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03889\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ remaining\ a\ true\ 64-\/bit/128-\/bit\ hash\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03890\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03891\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ is\ done\ by\ prioritizing\ a\ subset\ of\ 64-\/bit\ operations\ that\ can\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03892\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ emulated\ without\ too\ many\ steps\ on\ the\ average\ 32-\/bit\ machine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03893\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03894\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ example,\ these\ two\ lines\ seem\ similar,\ and\ run\ equally\ fast\ on\ 64-\/bit:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03895\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03896\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ xxh\_u64\ x;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03897\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x\ \string^=\ (x\ >>\ 47);\ //\ good}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03898\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x\ \string^=\ (x\ >>\ 13);\ //\ bad}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03899\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03900\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ to\ a\ 32-\/bit\ machine,\ there\ is\ a\ major\ difference.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03901\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03902\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ x\ \string^=\ (x\ >>\ 47)\ looks\ like\ this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03903\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03904\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x.lo\ \string^=\ (x.hi\ >>\ (47\ -\/\ 32));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03905\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03906\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ while\ x\ \string^=\ (x\ >>\ 13)\ looks\ like\ this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03907\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03908\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ //\ note:\ funnel\ shifts\ are\ not\ usually\ cheap.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03909\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x.lo\ \string^=\ (x.lo\ >>\ 13)\ |\ (x.hi\ <<\ (32\ -\/\ 13));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03910\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x.hi\ \string^=\ (x.hi\ >>\ 13);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03911\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03912\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ first\ one\ is\ significantly\ faster\ than\ the\ second,\ simply\ because\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03913\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ shift\ is\ larger\ than\ 32.\ This\ means:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03914\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ All\ the\ bits\ we\ need\ are\ in\ the\ upper\ 32\ bits,\ so\ we\ can\ ignore\ the\ lower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03915\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ 32\ bits\ in\ the\ shift.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03916\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ The\ shift\ result\ will\ always\ fit\ in\ the\ lower\ 32\ bits,\ and\ therefore,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03917\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ we\ can\ ignore\ the\ upper\ 32\ bits\ in\ the\ xor.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03918\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03919\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Thanks\ to\ this\ optimization,\ XXH3\ only\ requires\ these\ features\ to\ be\ efficient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03920\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03921\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ Usable\ unaligned\ access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03922\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ A\ 32-\/bit\ or\ 64-\/bit\ ALU}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03923\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ If\ 32-\/bit,\ a\ decent\ ADC\ instruction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03924\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ A\ 32\ or\ 64-\/bit\ multiply\ with\ a\ 64-\/bit\ result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03925\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ For\ the\ 128-\/bit\ variant,\ a\ decent\ byteswap\ helps\ short\ inputs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03926\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03927\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ first\ two\ are\ already\ required\ by\ XXH32,\ and\ almost\ all\ 32-\/bit\ and\ 64-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03928\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ platforms\ which\ can\ run\ XXH32\ can\ run\ XXH3\ efficiently.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03929\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03930\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Thumb-\/1,\ the\ classic\ 16-\/bit\ only\ subset\ of\ ARM's\ instruction\ set,\ is\ one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03931\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ notable\ exception.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03932\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03933\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ First\ of\ all,\ Thumb-\/1\ lacks\ support\ for\ the\ UMULL\ instruction\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03934\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ performs\ the\ important\ long\ multiply.\ This\ means\ numerous\ \_\_aeabi\_lmul}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03935\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03936\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03937\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Second\ of\ all,\ the\ 8\ functional\ registers\ are\ just\ not\ enough.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03938\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Setup\ for\ \_\_aeabi\_lmul,\ byteshift\ loads,\ pointers,\ and\ all\ arithmetic\ need}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03939\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Lo\ registers,\ and\ this\ shuffling\ results\ in\ thousands\ more\ MOVs\ than\ A32.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03940\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03941\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ A32\ and\ T32\ don't\ have\ this\ limitation.\ They\ can\ access\ all\ 14\ registers,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03942\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ do\ a\ 32-\/>64\ multiply\ with\ UMULL,\ and\ the\ flexible\ operand\ allowing\ free}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03943\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ shifts\ is\ helpful,\ too.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03944\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03945\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Therefore,\ we\ do\ a\ quick\ sanity\ check.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03946\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03947\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ compiling\ Thumb-\/1\ for\ a\ target\ which\ supports\ ARM\ instructions,\ we\ will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03948\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ emit\ a\ warning,\ as\ it\ is\ not\ a\ "{}sane"{}\ platform\ to\ compile\ for.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03949\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03950\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Usually,\ if\ this\ happens,\ it\ is\ because\ of\ an\ accident\ and\ you\ probably\ need}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03951\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ to\ specify\ -\/march,\ as\ you\ likely\ meant\ to\ compile\ for\ a\ newer\ architecture.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03952\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03953\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Credit:\ large\ sections\ of\ the\ vectorial\ and\ asm\ source\ code\ paths}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03954\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ have\ been\ contributed\ by\ @easyaspi314}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03955\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03956\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_\_thumb\_\_)\ \&\&\ !defined(\_\_thumb2\_\_)\ \&\&\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH\_ISA\_ARM)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03957\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ warning\ "{}XXH3\ is\ highly\ inefficient\ without\ ARM\ or\ Thumb-\/2."{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03958\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03959\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{03960\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ ==========================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03961\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Vectorization\ detection}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03962\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ==========================================\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03963\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{03994\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ defined(\_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_ARM\_NEON)\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ gcc\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04083\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04084\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ UGLY\ HACK:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04085\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ GCC\ usually\ generates\ the\ best\ code\ with\ -\/O3\ for\ xxHash.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04086\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04087\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ when\ targeting\ AVX2,\ it\ is\ overzealous\ in\ its\ unrolling\ resulting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ in\ code\ roughly\ 3/4\ the\ speed\ of\ Clang.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04089\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04090\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ There\ are\ other\ issues,\ such\ as\ GCC\ splitting\ \_mm256\_loadu\_si256\ into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04091\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_mm\_loadu\_si128\ +\ \_mm256\_inserti128\_si256.\ This\ is\ an\ optimization\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04092\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ only\ applies\ to\ Sandy\ and\ Ivy\ Bridge...\ which\ don't\ even\ support\ AVX2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04093\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04094\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ That\ is\ why\ when\ compiling\ the\ AVX2\ version,\ it\ is\ recommended\ to\ use\ either}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04095\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ -\/O2\ -\/mavx2\ -\/march=haswell}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04096\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04097\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ -\/O2\ -\/mavx2\ -\/mno-\/avx256-\/split-\/unaligned-\/load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04098\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ for\ decent\ performance,\ or\ to\ use\ Clang\ instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04099\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04100\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Fortunately,\ we\ can\ control\ the\ first\ one\ with\ a\ pragma\ that\ forces\ GCC\ into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04101\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/O2,\ but\ the\ other\ one\ we\ can't\ control\ without\ "{}failed\ to\ inline\ always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04102\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ inline\ function\ due\ to\ target\ mismatch"{}\ warnings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04103\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04104\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ XXH\_VECTOR\ ==\ XXH\_AVX2\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ AVX2\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04640\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ ==========================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04641\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Short\ keys}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04642\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ==========================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04643\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ One\ of\ the\ shortcomings\ of\ XXH32\ and\ XXH64\ was\ that\ their\ performance\ was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04644\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ sub-\/optimal\ on\ short\ lengths.\ It\ used\ an\ iterative\ algorithm\ which\ strongly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04645\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ favored\ lengths\ that\ were\ a\ multiple\ of\ 4\ or\ 8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04646\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04647\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Instead\ of\ iterating\ over\ individual\ inputs,\ we\ use\ a\ set\ of\ single\ shot}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04648\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ functions\ which\ piece\ together\ a\ range\ of\ lengths\ and\ operate\ in\ constant\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04649\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04650\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Additionally,\ the\ number\ of\ multiplies\ has\ been\ significantly\ reduced.\ This}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04652\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04660\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04739\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04740\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ DISCLAIMER:\ There\ are\ known\ *seed-\/dependent*\ multicollisions\ here\ due\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04741\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ multiplication\ by\ zero,\ affecting\ hashes\ of\ lengths\ 17\ to\ 240.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04742\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04743\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ they\ are\ very\ unlikely.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04744\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04745\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Keep\ this\ in\ mind\ when\ using\ the\ unseeded\ XXH3\_64bits()\ variant:\ As\ with\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04746\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ unseeded\ non-\/cryptographic\ hashes,\ it\ does\ not\ attempt\ to\ defend\ itself}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04747\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ against\ specially\ crafted\ inputs,\ only\ random\ inputs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04748\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04749\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Compared\ to\ classic\ UMAC\ where\ a\ 1\ in\ 2\string^31\ chance\ of\ 4\ consecutive\ bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04750\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ cancelling\ out\ the\ secret\ is\ taken\ an\ arbitrary\ number\ of\ times\ (addressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04751\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ in\ XXH3\_accumulate\_512),\ this\ collision\ is\ very\ unlikely\ with\ random\ inputs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04752\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and/or\ proper\ seeding:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04753\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04754\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ only\ has\ a\ 1\ in\ 2\string^63\ chance\ of\ 8\ consecutive\ bytes\ cancelling\ out,\ in\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04755\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ function\ that\ is\ only\ called\ up\ to\ 16\ times\ per\ hash\ with\ up\ to\ 240\ bytes\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04756\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04757\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04758\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ is\ not\ too\ bad\ for\ a\ non-\/cryptographic\ hash\ function,\ especially\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04759\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ only\ 64\ bit\ outputs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04760\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04761\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ 128-\/bit\ variant\ (which\ trades\ some\ speed\ for\ strength)\ is\ NOT\ affected}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04762\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ by\ this,\ although\ it\ is\ always\ a\ good\ idea\ to\ use\ a\ proper\ seed\ if\ you\ care}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04763\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ about\ strength.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04764\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04967\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04968\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH3\_accumulate\_512\ is\ the\ tightest\ loop\ for\ long\ inputs,\ and\ it\ is\ the\ most\ optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04969\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04970\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ It\ is\ a\ hardened\ version\ of\ UMAC,\ based\ off\ of\ FARSH's\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04971\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04972\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ was\ chosen\ because\ it\ adapts\ quite\ well\ to\ 32-\/bit,\ 64-\/bit,\ and\ SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04973\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ implementations,\ and\ it\ is\ ridiculously\ fast.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04974\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04975\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ We\ harden\ it\ by\ mixing\ the\ original\ input\ to\ the\ accumulators\ as\ well\ as\ the\ product.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04976\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04977\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ means\ that\ in\ the\ (relatively\ likely)\ case\ of\ a\ multiply\ by\ zero,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04978\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ original\ input\ is\ preserved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04979\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04980\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ On\ 128-\/bit\ inputs,\ we\ swap\ 64-\/bit\ pairs\ when\ we\ add\ the\ input\ to\ improve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04981\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ cross-\/pollination,\ as\ otherwise\ the\ upper\ and\ lower\ halves\ would\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04982\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ essentially\ independent.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04983\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04984\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ doesn't\ matter\ on\ 64-\/bit\ hashes\ since\ they\ all\ get\ merged\ together\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04985\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ end,\ so\ we\ skip\ the\ extra\ step.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04986\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04987\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Both\ XXH3\_64bits\ and\ XXH3\_128bits\ use\ this\ subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04988\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04989\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{05026\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH3\_scrambleAcc:\ Scrambles\ the\ accumulators\ to\ improve\ mixing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Multiplication\ isn't\ perfect,\ as\ explained\ by\ Google\ in\ HighwayHash:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05030\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ //\ Multiplication\ mixes/scrambles\ bytes\ 0-\/7\ of\ the\ 64-\/bit\ result\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ //\ varying\ degrees.\ In\ descending\ order\ of\ goodness,\ bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ //\ 3\ 4\ 2\ 5\ 1\ 6\ 0\ 7\ have\ quality\ 228\ 224\ 164\ 160\ 100\ 96\ 36\ 32.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05034\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ //\ As\ expected,\ the\ upper\ and\ lower\ bytes\ are\ much\ worse.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05035\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Source:\ https://github.com/google/highwayhash/blob/0aaf66b/highwayhash/hh\_avx2.h\#L291}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Since\ our\ algorithm\ uses\ a\ pseudorandom\ secret\ to\ add\ some\ variance\ into\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ mix,\ we\ don't\ need\ to\ (or\ want\ to)\ mix\ as\ often\ or\ as\ much\ as\ HighwayHash\ does.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ isn't\ as\ tight\ as\ XXH3\_accumulate,\ but\ still\ written\ in\ SIMD\ to\ avoid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ extraction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Both\ XXH3\_64bits\ and\ XXH3\_128bits\ use\ this\ subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05046\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{05971\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05972\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ In\ XXH3\_scalarRound(),\ GCC\ and\ Clang\ have\ a\ similar\ codegen\ issue,\ where\ they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05973\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ emit\ an\ excess\ mask\ and\ a\ full\ 64-\/bit\ multiply-\/add\ (MADD\ X-\/form).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05974\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05975\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ While\ this\ might\ not\ seem\ like\ much,\ as\ AArch64\ is\ a\ 64-\/bit\ architecture,\ only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05976\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ big\ Cortex\ designs\ have\ a\ full\ 64-\/bit\ multiplier.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05977\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05978\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ On\ the\ little\ cores,\ the\ smaller\ 32-\/bit\ multiplier\ is\ used,\ and\ full\ 64-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05979\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ multiplies\ expand\ to\ 2-\/3\ multiplies\ in\ microcode.\ This\ has\ a\ major\ penalty}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05980\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ of\ up\ to\ 4\ latency\ cycles\ and\ 2\ stall\ cycles\ in\ the\ multiply\ pipeline.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05981\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05982\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Thankfully,\ AArch64\ still\ provides\ the\ 32-\/bit\ long\ multiply-\/add\ (UMADDL)\ which\ does}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05983\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ not\ have\ this\ penalty\ and\ does\ the\ mask\ automatically.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05984\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06101\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06102\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ UGLY\ HACK:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06103\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ GCC\ and\ Clang\ generate\ a\ bunch\ of\ MOV/MOVK\ pairs\ for\ aarch64,\ and\ they\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06104\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ placed\ sequentially,\ in\ order,\ at\ the\ top\ of\ the\ unrolled\ loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06105\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06106\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ While\ MOVK\ is\ great\ for\ generating\ constants\ (2\ cycles\ for\ a\ 64-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06107\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ constant\ compared\ to\ 4\ cycles\ for\ LDR),\ it\ fights\ for\ bandwidth\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06108\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ the\ arithmetic\ instructions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06109\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06110\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ I\ \ \ L\ \ \ S}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06112\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ MOVK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06113\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ MOVK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06114\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ MOVK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06115\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ ADD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06116\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ SUB\ \ \ \ \ \ STR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06117\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ STR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06118\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ By\ forcing\ loads\ from\ memory\ (as\ the\ asm\ line\ causes\ the\ compiler\ to\ assume}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06119\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ that\ XXH3\_kSecretPtr\ has\ been\ changed),\ the\ pipelines\ are\ used\ more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06120\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ efficiently:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06121\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ I\ \ \ L\ \ \ S}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06122\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ LDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06123\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ ADD\ LDR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06124\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ SUB\ \ \ \ \ STR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06125\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ STR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06126\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ XXH3\_64bits\_withSeed,\ len\ ==\ 256,\ Snapdragon\ 835}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06138\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06355\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06356\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH3\_hashLong\_64b\_withSeed():}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06357\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Generate\ a\ custom\ key\ based\ on\ alteration\ of\ default\ XXH3\_kSecret\ with\ the\ seed,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06358\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ then\ use\ this\ key\ for\ long\ mode\ hashing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06359\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06360\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ operation\ is\ decently\ fast\ but\ nonetheless\ costs\ a\ little\ bit\ of\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06361\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Try\ to\ avoid\ it\ whenever\ possible\ (typically\ when\ seed==0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06362\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06363\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ It's\ important\ for\ performance\ that\ XXH3\_hashLong\ is\ not\ inlined.\ Not\ sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06364\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ why\ (uop\ cache\ maybe?),\ but\ the\ difference\ is\ large\ and\ easily\ measurable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06365\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06455\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{06456\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ ===\ \ \ XXH3\ streaming\ \ \ ===\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06457\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ XXH\_NO\_STREAM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06458\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06459\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Malloc's\ a\ pointer\ that\ is\ always\ aligned\ to\ @align.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06460\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06461\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ must\ be\ freed\ with\ \`{}XXH\_alignedFree()`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06462\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06463\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ malloc\ typically\ guarantees\ 16\ byte\ alignment\ on\ 64-\/bit\ systems\ and\ 8\ byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06464\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ alignment\ on\ 32-\/bit.\ This\ isn't\ enough\ for\ the\ 32\ byte\ aligned\ loads\ in\ AVX2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06465\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ or\ on\ 32-\/bit,\ the\ 16\ byte\ aligned\ loads\ in\ SSE2\ and\ NEON.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06466\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06467\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ underalignment\ previously\ caused\ a\ rather\ obvious\ crash\ which\ went}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06468\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ completely\ unnoticed\ due\ to\ XXH3\_createState()\ not\ actually\ being\ tested.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06469\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Credit\ to\ RedSpah\ for\ noticing\ this\ bug.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06470\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06471\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ alignment\ is\ done\ manually:\ Functions\ like\ posix\_memalign\ or\ \_mm\_malloc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06472\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ are\ avoided:\ To\ maintain\ portability,\ we\ would\ have\ to\ write\ a\ fallback}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06473\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ like\ this\ anyways,\ and\ besides,\ testing\ for\ the\ existence\ of\ library}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06474\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ functions\ without\ relying\ on\ external\ build\ tools\ is\ impossible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06475\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06476\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ method\ is\ simple:\ Overallocate,\ manually\ align,\ and\ store\ the\ offset}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06477\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ to\ the\ original\ behind\ the\ returned\ pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06478\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06479\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Align\ must\ be\ a\ power\ of\ 2\ and\ 8\ <=\ align\ <=\ 128.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06480\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06481\ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ XXH\_MALLOCF\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ XXH\_alignedMalloc(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ s,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ align)}
\DoxyCodeLine{06482\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{06483\ \ \ \ \ XXH\_ASSERT(align\ <=\ 128\ \&\&\ align\ >=\ 8);\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ range\ check\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06484\ \ \ \ \ XXH\_ASSERT((align\ \&\ (align-\/1))\ ==\ 0);\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ power\ of\ 2\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06485\ \ \ \ \ XXH\_ASSERT(s\ !=\ 0\ \&\&\ s\ <\ (s\ +\ align));\ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ empty/overflow\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06486\ \ \ \ \ \{\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Overallocate\ to\ make\ room\ for\ manual\ realignment\ and\ an\ offset\ byte\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06487\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xxh\_u8*\ base\ =\ (xxh\_u8*)XXH\_malloc(s\ +\ align);}
\DoxyCodeLine{06488\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (base\ !=\ NULL)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{06489\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06490\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ Get\ the\ offset\ needed\ to\ align\ this\ pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06491\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06492\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ Even\ if\ the\ returned\ pointer\ is\ aligned,\ there\ will\ always\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06493\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ at\ least\ one\ byte\ to\ store\ the\ offset\ to\ the\ original\ pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06494\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06495\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ offset\ =\ align\ -\/\ ((size\_t)base\ \&\ (align\ -\/\ 1));\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ base\ \%\ align\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06496\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Add\ the\ offset\ for\ the\ now-\/aligned\ pointer\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06497\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xxh\_u8*\ ptr\ =\ base\ +\ offset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{06498\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{06499\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ XXH\_ASSERT((\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})ptr\ \%\ align\ ==\ 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{06500\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{06501\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Store\ the\ offset\ immediately\ before\ the\ returned\ pointer.\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06502\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ptr[-\/1]\ =\ (xxh\_u8)offset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{06503\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ ptr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{06504\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06505\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{06506\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06507\ \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06853\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ ==========================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06854\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH3\ 128\ bits\ (a.k.a\ XXH128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06855\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ==========================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06856\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH3's\ 128-\/bit\ variant\ has\ better\ mixing\ and\ strength\ than\ the\ 64-\/bit\ variant,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06857\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ even\ without\ counting\ the\ significantly\ larger\ output\ size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06858\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06859\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ example,\ extra\ steps\ are\ taken\ to\ avoid\ the\ seed-\/dependent\ collisions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06860\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ in\ 17-\/240\ byte\ inputs\ (See\ XXH3\_mix16B\ and\ XXH128\_mix32B).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06861\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06862\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ strength\ naturally\ comes\ at\ the\ cost\ of\ some\ speed,\ especially\ on\ short}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06863\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ lengths.\ Note\ that\ longer\ hashes\ are\ about\ as\ fast\ as\ the\ 64-\/bit\ version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06864\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ due\ to\ it\ using\ only\ a\ slight\ modification\ of\ the\ 64-\/bit\ loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06865\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06866\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH128\ is\ also\ more\ oriented\ towards\ 64-\/bit\ machines.\ It\ is\ still\ extremely}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06867\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ fast\ for\ a\ \_128-\/bit\_\ hash\ on\ 32-\/bit\ (it\ usually\ clears\ XXH64).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06868\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
